CHI_integrate_the_warlords = { #整合军阀

	CHI_integrate_the_army = { #整合[From.GetAdjective]军队

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {

			FROM = { compare_autonomy_state < autonomy_colony }

			custom_trigger_tooltip = {

				tooltip = CHI_not_has_warlord_integration_maxed_out_tt

				NOT = {

					has_idea = CHI_warlord_integration_5

				}

			}

			#NOT = {

				#	has_country_flag = CHI_integrate_the_army

				#}

		}

		visible = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				has_country_flag = CHI_subjugate_warlords_flag

			}

			FROM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					has_country_flag = CHI_integrate_the_army

				}

			}

		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes



		cost = 150



		#MODDED VPI by Yard1

		target_array = subjects		

		#MODDED^ VPI by Yard1

		target_trigger = {

			FROM = {

				is_subject_of = ROOT

				is_warlord = yes

			}

		}

		days_remove = 70

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {

			factor = 10

			modifier = {

				OR = {

					has_idea = CHI_warlord_integration_3

					has_idea = CHI_warlord_integration_4

					has_idea = CHI_warlord_integration_5

				}

				factor = 0

				#TODO_WTT_CODE need a trigger for daily increase of PP to see if it's okay to reduce

			}

		}

		remove_effect = {

			add_command_power = 20

			FROM = {

				every_unit_leader = {

					limit = {

						OWNER = { TAG = THIS }

					}

					set_unit_leader_flag = allegiance_to_@FROM #return when wars break out

					set_nationality = ROOT

				}

				hidden_effect = {

					country_event = rcmchina.363 #notify them

				}

			}

			set_global_flag = joined_chi_@FROM

			FROM = { set_country_flag = CHI_integrate_the_army }

			custom_effect_tooltip = we_will_be_able_to_integrate_their_administration_tt

		}

		complete_effect = {

			CHI_warlord_integration_up = yes

		}

	}

	CHI_integrate_the_administration = { #整合[From.GetAdjective]政府

		}

	CHI_peace_with_wrl = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		available = {

	        OR = { 

				has_war_with = JAP

				JAP = { #日本

					focus_progress = {

					    focus = JAP_intervene_in_china

					    progress > 0.3

				   }

				}

			}

		}

		visible = {

			always = no ###EYWOR HAS THIS ALREADY, rcmchina.331 (event)

			hidden_trigger = {

			    any_enemy_country = {

				    is_literally_china = yes

			        NOT = { original_tag = SIK }

				    NOT = { is_subject_of = JAP }

					NOT = { has_civil_war = yes  }

			    }

			    NOT = {

					date > 1940.1.1

				}

			}

			NOT = {

				has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag

			}

             

		}

	

		cost = 35



		complete_effect = {

			every_enemy_country = {

                limit = {

					is_literally_china = yes

				    NOT = { original_tag = SIK }

				    NOT = { is_subject_of = JAP }

					NOT = { has_civil_war = yes  }

					is_in_faction = no

				}

				country_event = gxc.27

			}

			every_enemy_country = {

                limit = {

					is_literally_china = yes

					NOT = { original_tag = SIK }

				    NOT = { is_subject_of = JAP }

					NOT = { has_civil_war = yes  }

					OR = {

                        AND = {

							is_in_faction = yes

							all_allied_country = {

								is_ai = yes

							}

							is_faction_leader = yes

						}

						AND = {

							is_in_faction = yes

							is_faction_leader = no

							is_ai = no

							any_allied_country = {

								is_faction_leader = yes

								is_ai = yes

							}

						}

						AND = {

							is_in_faction = yes

							is_faction_leader = yes

							is_ai = no

						}

					}

				}

				country_event = gxc.27

			}

		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {

			factor = 5000

		}

	}

}

CHI_xian_incident = { #西安事变

		CHI_instigate_xian_incident = { #发动西安事变

			icon = generic_political_discourse

			available = {

				#NOT ={	# MODDED

				#	PRC = {

				#		has_completed_focus = PRC_Anti_Japanese_and_Chiang

				#	}

				#}

				NOT = {

					JAP = { #日本

						has_global_flag = kodoha_won

					}

				}

				has_global_flag = tacit_truce_flag

				OR = {

					has_government = democratic

					has_government = neutrality

				}

				CHI = { #中国

					#has_opinion_modifier = hostile_status

					NOT = { has_war_with = GXC }

					NOT = { has_global_flag = CHI_truce_com }

					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }

				}

				has_global_flag = chiang_in_xian

				country_exists = PRC

				NOT = {

					has_global_flag = CHI_xian_fired

				}

				NOT = {

					has_opinion_modifier = CHI_prc_reconciliation

				}

				NOT = {

					has_war_with = CHI 

				}

			}

			visible = {

				country_exists = PRC

				has_country_flag = I_can_do_xian_incident

				tag = NEA

			}

			cancel_trigger = {

				OR = {

				    NOT = {

					   country_exists = PRC

				    }

					has_war_with = CHI 

					hidden_trigger = { has_global_flag = NEA_choose_xian_incident_happen } #guo

				}

			}

			#cost = 10

			ai_will_do = {

	WTT_escalate_incident_to_border_conflict = {

			}

		}

					on_lose = wtt_border_conflict_lost_attacker.1

					on_cancel = wtt_border_conflict_canceled_attacker.1

				}



				defender = {

					state = var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT

					num_provinces = 4

					on_win = wtt_border_conflict_won_defender.1

					on_lose = wtt_border_conflict_lost_defender.1

					on_cancel = wtt_border_conflict_canceled_defender.1

			}

			activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = WTT_border_conflict_time_until_cancelled }

		}

		icon = decision_generic_ignite_civil_war

		visible = {

			}

		}

			if = {

				limit = { is_border_conflict_defender_vs_FROM = yes }

				var:ROOT.defender_state_vs_@FROM = { save_event_target_as = their_state }

				var:ROOT.attacker_state_vs_@FROM = { save_event_target_as = our_state }

			}

			else = {

				var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT = { save_event_target_as = our_state }

				var:FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT = { save_event_target_as = their_state }

			}

			FROM = {

				country_event = { id = wtt_border_conflict_escalate_to_war.1 }

				hidden_effect = {

					remove_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = WTT_border_conflict_escalate_to_war }

				}

		 	}

		}



		remove_effect = {

			cancel_border_war = {

				dont_fire_events = yes

				defender = var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT

				attacker = var:FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT

			}

			declare_war_on = { target = FROM type = annex_everything }

			if = {

				limit = { is_border_conflict_defender_vs_FROM = yes }

				var:attacker_state_vs_@FROM = {

					clr_state_flag = border_incident_active

				}

				var:defender_state_vs_@FROM = {

					clr_state_flag = border_incident_active

				}

				clear_variable = attacker_state_vs_@FROM

				clear_variable = defender_state_vs_@FROM

			}

			else = {

				FROM = {

					var:attacker_state_vs_@ROOT = {

						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active

					}

					var:defender_state_vs_@ROOT = {

						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active

					}

					clear_variable = attacker_state_vs_@ROOT

					clear_variable = defender_state_vs_@ROOT

				}

			}

		}

	}

					attacker = FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT

					defender = FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT

					defender_win = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

				}

			}

			else = {

				custom_effect_tooltip = WTT_national_leadership_effect_tooltip_leader

				effect_tooltip = {

					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { add_ideas = CHI_illegal_regime }

				}

			}

		}

	}

	#Nat China



	#595 "Fukien"	#MODDED

	WTT_build_support_in_fujian = { #在福建地区建立支持§G([?595.state_political_support_value|+0])§!

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_COST_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		visible = {

			595 = {

				WTT_should_show_state_decision = yes

			}

			WTT_show_build_support_decisions = yes

		}



		available = {

			595 = {

				WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

			}

		}



		cancel_trigger = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					595 = {

						WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

					}

				}

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_GAIN_SUPPORT

		}



		days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 595

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Another country has majority in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				any_other_country = {

					595 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					595 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#I am super far ahead

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				set_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					595 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 595.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 595.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				595 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					595 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 595.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 595.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					595 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 595.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				595 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 595.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 595.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				595 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 595.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 595.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall #factor doesn't work with add

			modifier = {

				factor = 0.9

				always = yes

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				factor = 0.3 #1.11 MODDED og was 0.6

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				factor = 1.2

				strength_ratio = {

    					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

    					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				factor = 1.2

				strength_ratio = {

    					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

    					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#tone down if not bordered

			modifier = {

				factor = 0.5

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				factor = 3

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				factor = 0.8

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				factor = 0.8

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				factor = 0

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.5

				}

			}

			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			595 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 597.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 597.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			597 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}



	#1015 "Jiangsu"

	WTT_build_support_in_jiangsu = { #在江苏地区建立支持§G([?598.state_political_support_value|+0])§!

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_COST_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		visible = {

			1015 = {

				WTT_should_show_state_decision = yes

			}

			WTT_show_build_support_decisions = yes

		}



		available = {

			1015 = {

				WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

			}

		}



		cancel_trigger = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					1015 = {

						WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

					}

				}

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_GAIN_SUPPORT

		}



		days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 1015

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Another country has majority in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				any_other_country = {

					1015 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					1015 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#I am super far ahead

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				set_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					1015 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 1015.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 1015.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				1015 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					1015 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 1015.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 1015.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					1015 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 1015.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				1015 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 1015.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 1015.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				1015 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 1015.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 1015.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 1015.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

				}

			}

				}

			}

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				1042 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 1042.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 1042.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 1042.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong 	#MODDEDvvvv

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

				#MODDED^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			1042 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}



	#602 "Hunan"

	WTT_build_support_in_hunan = { #在湖南地区建立支持§G([?602.state_political_support_value|+0])§!

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_COST_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		visible = {

			602 = {

				WTT_should_show_state_decision = yes

			}

			WTT_show_build_support_decisions = yes

		}



		available = {

			602 = {

				WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

			}

		}



		cancel_trigger = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					602 = {

						WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

					}

				}

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_GAIN_SUPPORT

		}



		days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 602

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Another country has majority in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				any_other_country = {

					602 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					602 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#I am super far ahead

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				set_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					602 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 602.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 602.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				602 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					602 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 602.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 602.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					602 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 602.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				602 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 602.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 602.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				602 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 602.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 602.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 602.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				605 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 605.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 605.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				605 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 605.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 605.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 605.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			605 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}



	#749 "Anhui"

	WTT_build_support_in_anhui = { #在安徽地区建立支持§G([?606.state_political_support_value|+0])§!

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_COST_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		visible = {

			749 = {

				WTT_should_show_state_decision = yes

			}

			WTT_show_build_support_decisions = yes

		}



		available = {

			749 = {

				WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

			}

		}



		cancel_trigger = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					749 = {

						WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

					}

				}

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_GAIN_SUPPORT

		}



		days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 749

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



		#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Another country has majority in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				any_other_country = {

					749 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					749 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#I am super far ahead

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				set_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					749 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 749.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 749.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				749 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					749 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 749.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 749.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					749 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 749.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				749 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 749.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 749.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				749 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 749.political_platform_@PREV }

				}

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 608.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				608 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 608.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 608.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				608 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 608.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 608.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 608.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			608 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}



	#613 "Shanghai"

	WTT_build_support_in_shanghai = { #在上海建立支持§G([?613.state_political_support_value|+0])§!

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_COST_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		visible = {

			613 = {

				WTT_should_show_state_decision = yes

			}

			WTT_show_build_support_decisions = yes

		}



		available = {

			613 = {

				WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

			}

		}



		cancel_trigger = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					613 = {

						WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

					}

				}

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_GAIN_SUPPORT

		}



		days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 613

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Another country has majority in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				any_other_country = {

					613 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					613 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#I am super far ahead

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				set_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					613 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 613.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 613.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				613 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					613 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 613.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 613.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					613 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 620.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					620 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 620.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				620 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 620.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 620.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				620 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 620.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 620.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 620.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			620 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

	#615 "Shanxi"

	WTT_build_support_in_shanxi = { #在山西地区建立支持§G([?615.state_political_support_value|+0])§!

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_COST_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		visible = {

			615 = {

				WTT_should_show_state_decision = yes

			}

			WTT_show_build_support_decisions = yes

		}



		available = {

			615 = {

				WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

			}

		}



		cancel_trigger = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					615 = {

						WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

					}

				}

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_GAIN_SUPPORT

		}



		days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 615

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Another country has majority in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				any_other_country = {

					615 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					615 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#I am super far ahead

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				set_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					615 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 615.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 615.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				615 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					615 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 615.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 615.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					615 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					622 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 622.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 622.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					622 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 622.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				622 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 622.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 622.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				622 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 622.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 622.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 622.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			622 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

	#283 "Gansu"

	WTT_build_support_in_gansu = { #在甘肃地区建立支持§G([?283.state_political_support_value|+0])§!

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_COST_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		visible = {

			283 = { #士兵在前进

				WTT_should_show_state_decision = yes

			}

			WTT_show_build_support_decisions = yes

		}



		available = {

			283 = { #士兵在前进

				WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

			}

		}



		cancel_trigger = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					283 = { #士兵在前进

						WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

					}

				}

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_GAIN_SUPPORT

		}



		days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 283

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Another country has majority in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				any_other_country = {

					283 = { #士兵在前进

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

					}

				}

			}

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					283 = { #士兵在前进

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 283.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 283.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				283 = { #士兵在前进

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					616 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 616.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 616.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				616 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					616 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 616.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 616.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					616 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 616.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				616 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 616.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 616.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				616 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 616.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 616.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 616.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			616 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

					}

				}

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					760 = {	#MODDED

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#I am super far ahead

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				set_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					760 = {	#MODDED

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 760.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 760.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				760 = {	#MODDED

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					760 = {	#MODDED

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 760.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 760.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					760 = {	#MODDED

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 760.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				760 = {	#MODDED

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 760.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 760.political_platform_@THIS }	#MODDED

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				760 = {	#MODDED

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 760.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 760.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }	#MODDED

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 760.political_platform_@THIS }	#MODDED

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}

		#MODDEDvvvvvvvvvvvvvvvvvvvvv

		remove_effect = {

			760 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}

					#MODDED^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

	#Guangxi Clique



	#591 "Hainan"

	WTT_build_support_in_hainan = { #在海南建立支持§G([?591.state_political_support_value|+0])§!

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_COST_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED

		icon = generic_political_discourse

		visible = {

			591 = {

				WTT_should_show_state_decision = yes

			}

			WTT_show_build_support_decisions = yes

		}



		available = {

			591 = {

				WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

			}

		}



		cancel_trigger = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				NOT = {

					591 = {

						WTT_can_ROOT_select_state_support_decision_state = yes

					}

				}

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_GAIN_SUPPORT

		}



		days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 591

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Another country has majority in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				any_other_country = {

					591 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					}

				}

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					591 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#I am super far ahead

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				set_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				add_to_temp_variable = { temp_support_points = -40 }

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						check_variable = { total_political_support_points > temp_support_points }

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Focus elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -45

				any_other_country = {

					591 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead > 4 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				591 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#I have a change to grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					591 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < 2 }

			}



			#I can for sure grab this with just one push for support

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				any_other_country = {

					591 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_points = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { points_difference = majority_holder_points }

				check_variable = { points_difference < 1 }

			}



			#I am far enough ahead in this state

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				591 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 595.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 591.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }



				check_variable = { my_points_lead > 2 }

			}



			#I want to push just a little bit ahead of my opponent so he cannot grab state

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				591 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 591.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 591.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}



			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#BUILD_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			591 = {

				#Add random state support for ROOT

				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

					#Update state support

					#Status events

					#Recalc all support

				}

			}

		}
