					#Status events

					WTT_fire_remove_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}



	#1045 "Xining"

	WTT_remove_opposition_in_qinghai = { #清除在青海的反对派

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		icon = oppression

		visible = {

			WTT_is_ROOT_current_leader_of_china = yes

			1045 = {

				WTT_can_select_state_remove_support_state = yes

			}

		}



		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_REMOVE_OPPOSITION_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED



		available = {

			1045 = {

				WTT_can_select_state_remove_support_state = yes

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_REMOVE_OPPOSITION

		}





		days_remove = global.days_remove_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_REMOVE_SUPPORT

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 1045

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#REMOVE_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Rarely worth it if we have majority

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				1045 = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					1045 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#No other country has support in this state 	#MODDED?

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						1045 = {

							check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

						}

					}

				}

			}

			

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				check_variable = {

					Root.other_political_support < -2 #too much neg points!

				}

			}

				#MODDED^^^?



			#If I am close to losing... cut my life into pieces...

			modifier = {

				add = 75

				set_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = { check_variable = { total_political_support_points > highest_opposition_support_points } }

						set_temp_variable = { highest_opposition_support_points = total_political_support_points }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = highest_opposition_support_points }

				check_variable = { my_support_point_lead < 10 }

			}



			#Opponent has enough points that I need to be scared

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				set_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = { check_variable = { total_political_support_points > highest_opposition_support_points } }

						set_temp_variable = { highest_opposition_support_points = total_political_support_points }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = highest_opposition_support_points }

				check_variable = { my_support_point_lead < 20 }

			}



			#I will grab this state if I stomp out the opposition

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}





				any_other_country = {

					1045 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = STATE_ID.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 1045.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < support_to_remove }

			}



			#It is not worth the points

			modifier = {

				add = -50



				#Don't calc this for own states

				1045 = { NOT = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV } }



				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}



				check_variable = { support_to_remove < 1045.political_platform_@PREV }

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Stomp elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}





				any_other_country = {

					1045 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 1045.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 1045.political_platform_@PREV }

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = support_to_remove }



				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal > 3 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				1045 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is too close for my liking

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				1045 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 1045.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 1045.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 1045.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}

			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#REMOVE_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			1045 = {

				custom_effect_tooltip = state_majority_country_rules

				custom_effect_tooltip = state_support_breakdown

				custom_effect_tooltip = remove_support_in_state_chance_modifiers



				#Remove support from opposition

				WTT_remove_opposition_state_support = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_remove_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 1049.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < support_to_remove }

			}



			#It is not worth the points

			modifier = {

				add = -50



				#Don't calc this for own states

				1049 = { NOT = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV } }	#MODDED



				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}



				check_variable = { support_to_remove < 1049.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Stomp elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}





				any_other_country = {

					1049 = {	#MODDED

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 1049.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 1049.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = support_to_remove }



				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal > 3 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				1049 = {	#MODDED

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is too close for my liking

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				1049 = {	#MODDED

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 1049.political_platform_@PREV }	#MODDED

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 1049.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }	#MODDED

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 1049.political_platform_@THIS }	#MODDED

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}

			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#REMOVE_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END

		}



		remove_effect = {

			1049 = {	#MODDED

				custom_effect_tooltip = state_majority_country_rules

				custom_effect_tooltip = state_support_breakdown

				custom_effect_tooltip = remove_support_in_state_chance_modifiers



				#Remove support from opposition

				WTT_remove_opposition_state_support = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_remove_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

				hidden_effect = {

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

	WTT_remove_opposition_in_yarkand = { #清除在莎车的反对派

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		icon = oppression

		visible = {

			WTT_is_ROOT_current_leader_of_china = yes

			619 = {

				WTT_can_select_state_remove_support_state = yes

			}

		}



		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > @PP_GAIN_PER_DAY_REMOVE_OPPOSITION_TRIGGER

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_035	#MODDED



		available = {

			619 = {

				WTT_can_select_state_remove_support_state = yes

			}

		}



		modifier = {

			political_power_gain = @PP_COST_PER_DAY_REMOVE_OPPOSITION

		}





		days_remove = global.days_remove_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_REMOVE_SUPPORT

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 619

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#REMOVE_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Rarely worth it if we have majority

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				619 = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					619 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#No other country has support in this state 	#MODDED?

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						619 = {

							check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

						}

					}

				}

			}

			

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				check_variable = {

					Root.other_political_support < -2 #too much neg points!

				}

			}

				#MODDED^^^?



			#If I am close to losing... cut my life into pieces...

			modifier = {

				add = 75

				set_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = { check_variable = { total_political_support_points > highest_opposition_support_points } }

						set_temp_variable = { highest_opposition_support_points = total_political_support_points }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = highest_opposition_support_points }

				check_variable = { my_support_point_lead < 10 }

			}



			#Opponent has enough points that I need to be scared

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				set_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = { check_variable = { total_political_support_points > highest_opposition_support_points } }

						set_temp_variable = { highest_opposition_support_points = total_political_support_points }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = highest_opposition_support_points }

				check_variable = { my_support_point_lead < 20 }

			}



			#I will grab this state if I stomp out the opposition

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}





				any_other_country = {

					619 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = STATE_ID.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 619.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < support_to_remove }

			}



			#It is not worth the points

			modifier = {

				add = -50



				#Don't calc this for own states

				619 = { NOT = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV } }



				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}



				check_variable = { support_to_remove < 619.political_platform_@PREV }

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Stomp elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}





				any_other_country = {

					619 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 619.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 619.political_platform_@PREV }

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = support_to_remove }



				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal > 3 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				619 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is too close for my liking

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				619 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 619.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 619.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 619.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}

			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				}

			}

			}

			#MODDED^^^?



			#If I am close to losing... cut my life into pieces...

			modifier = {

				add = 75

				set_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = { check_variable = { total_political_support_points > highest_opposition_support_points } }

						set_temp_variable = { highest_opposition_support_points = total_political_support_points }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = highest_opposition_support_points }

				check_variable = { my_support_point_lead < 10 }

			}



			#Opponent has enough points that I need to be scared

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				set_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = { check_variable = { total_political_support_points > highest_opposition_support_points } }

						set_temp_variable = { highest_opposition_support_points = total_political_support_points }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = highest_opposition_support_points }

				check_variable = { my_support_point_lead < 20 }

			}



			#I will grab this state if I stomp out the opposition

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}





				any_other_country = {

					591 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = STATE_ID.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < support_to_remove }

			}



			#It is not worth the points

			modifier = {

				add = -50



				#Don't calc this for own states

				591 = { NOT = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV } }



				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}



				check_variable = { support_to_remove < 591.political_platform_@PREV }

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Stomp elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}





				any_other_country = {

					591 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = support_to_remove }



				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal > 3 }

			}



			#Big states are more important

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				591 = {

					check_variable = {

						var = state_political_support_value

						compare = greater_than_or_equals

						value = global.big_state_support_value

					}

				}

			}



			#Opponent is too close for my liking

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				591 = {

					has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 591.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 591.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 591.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}

			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#REMOVE_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END



		complete_effect = {



		}



		remove_effect = {

			591 = {

				custom_effect_tooltip = state_majority_country_rules

				custom_effect_tooltip = state_support_breakdown

				custom_effect_tooltip = remove_support_in_state_chance_modifiers



				#Remove support from opposition

				WTT_remove_opposition_state_support = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_remove_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	}

					if = {

						limit = {

							check_variable = { 593.political_platform_@THIS > closest_points }

						}

						set_temp_variable = { closest_points = 593.political_platform_@THIS }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = closest_points }

				check_variable = { my_points_lead < 2 }

			}

			#MODDEDv Tone down AI willingness overall

			modifier = {

				add = -15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#MODDED tone down even more for historical_ai

			modifier = {

				add = -55

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 20

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {					

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.4

				}

			}

			#strengthen if we are strong

			modifier = {

				add = 15

				NOT = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				strength_ratio = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					ratio = 0.7

				}

			}

			#block if not bordered

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

			}

			#BOOST IT IF IS LEADER SO AI WARLORDS DON'T TAKE OVER OFTEN

			modifier = {

				add = 35

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			#tone down if not a lot PP

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 1

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -35

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.7

				}

			}

			modifier = {

				add = -195

				NOT = {

					political_power_growth > 0.8

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^^

		}

#REMOVE_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_END

		}



		remove_effect = {

			593 = {

				custom_effect_tooltip = state_majority_country_rules

				custom_effect_tooltip = state_support_breakdown

				custom_effect_tooltip = remove_support_in_state_chance_modifiers



				#Remove support from opposition

				WTT_remove_opposition_state_support = yes



				hidden_effect = {

					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support

					save_event_target_as = state

					random_country = {

						limit = {

							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

						}

						save_event_target_as = majority_country

					}



					#Update state support

					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes



					#Status events

					WTT_fire_remove_support_status_events = yes



					#Recalc all support

					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

				}

			}

		}

	WTT_remove_opposition_in_nanning = { #清除在南宁的反对派

		on_map_mode = map_only #MODDED

		icon = oppression

		visible = {

		days_re_enable = 0



		cost = 0



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_state_targets = {

				state = 594

			}

		}



		fixed_random_seed = no



#REMOVE_SUPPORT_AI_WIL_DO_START

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0



			#Rarely worth it if we have majority

			modifier = {

				add = -50

				594 = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }

			}



			#Another country has some support in this state

			modifier = {

				add = 10

				any_other_country = {

					594 = {

						check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

					}

				}

			}



			#No other country has support in this state 	#MODDED?

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				NOT = {

					any_other_country = {

						594 = {

							check_variable = { political_platform_@PREV > 0 }

						}

					}

				}

			}

			

			modifier = {

				add = -100

				check_variable = {

					Root.other_political_support < -2 #too much neg points!

				}

			}

			#MODDED^^^?



			#If I am close to losing... cut my life into pieces...

			modifier = {

				add = 75

				set_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = { check_variable = { total_political_support_points > highest_opposition_support_points } }

						set_temp_variable = { highest_opposition_support_points = total_political_support_points }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = highest_opposition_support_points }

				check_variable = { my_support_point_lead < 10 }

			}



			#Opponent has enough points that I need to be scared

			modifier = {

				add = 25

				set_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = ROOT.total_political_support_points }

				all_other_country = {

					if = {

						limit = { check_variable = { total_political_support_points > highest_opposition_support_points } }

						set_temp_variable = { highest_opposition_support_points = total_political_support_points }

					}

				}

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { my_support_point_lead = highest_opposition_support_points }

				check_variable = { my_support_point_lead < 20 }

			}



			#I will grab this state if I stomp out the opposition

			modifier = {

				add = 50

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}





				any_other_country = {

					594 = {

						has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV

						set_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = STATE_ID.political_platform_@PREV }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead = 594.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead < support_to_remove }

			}



			#It is not worth the points

			modifier = {

				add = -50



				#Don't calc this for own states

				594 = { NOT = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV } }



				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

				if = {

					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = prince_of_terror }

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 2 }

				}

				if = {

					limit = {

						has_idea_with_trait = backroom_backstabber

					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 1 }

				}



				check_variable = { support_to_remove < 594.political_platform_@PREV }

			}



			#Opponent is far ahead in state. Stomp elsewhere first

			modifier = {

				add = -25

				set_temp_variable = { support_to_remove = 3 }

					}

				}



				subtract_from_temp_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal = 594.political_platform_@PREV }

				check_variable = { majority_holder_lead_after_removal > 3 }

					}

				}

			}

					set_temp_variable = { my_points_lead = 594.political_platform_@PREV }

				}



				all_other_country = {

RCM_remove_CC_and_BS = { #使极右翼组织制度化

	RCM_remove_CC_decision = { #使中央俱乐部集团制度化

		icon = generic_political_actions

		custom_cost_trigger = {

			political_power_growth > 0.5

		}

		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_05

		allowed = {

			tag = CHI

		}

		days_remove = 60

		visible = {

			OR = {

				has_idea = central_club

				has_idea = central_club_stronger

			}

			has_government = democratic

			has_completed_focus = CHI_lighthouse_of_democracy_focus

		}

		available = {

			hidden_trigger = {

				political_power_growth > 0.5

			}

		}

		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection



		}

		remove_trigger = { #will run remove effect and abort



		}

		remove_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_idea = central_club

				}

				remove_ideas = central_club

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					has_idea = central_club_stronger

				}

				remove_ideas = central_club_stronger

			}

		}

				limit = {

					FROM = {

						is_core_of = event_target:WTT_communist_china

						is_core_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					}

					

				}

				event_target:WTT_communist_china = {

					FROM = {

						state_event = { id = northeast_takeover.4 trigger_for = PREV }

					}

				}

				event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {

					FROM = {

						state_event = { id = northeast_takeover.34 trigger_for = PREV }

					}

				}

				FROM = {

					remove_core_of = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = increase_garrison_tt

				custom_effect_tooltip = decrease_garrison_com_good

			}

			else_if = {

				limit = {

					FROM = {

						NOT = {

							is_core_of = event_target:WTT_communist_china

						}

						is_core_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					}

				}

				event_target:WTT_communist_china = {

					FROM = {

						state_event = { id = northeast_takeover.6 trigger_for = PREV }

					}

				}

				event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {

					FROM = {

						state_event = { id = northeast_takeover.56 trigger_for = PREV }

					}

				}					

				FROM = {

					set_state_flag = strong_kmt_garrison		

				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = increase_garrison_tt

				custom_effect_tooltip = com_can_no_longer_influence

			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = troops_spawn_ccw_tt

		}

	}

}

				}

				activate_mission = chi_inner_mon_offensive_mission

			}

					limit = {

						region = 244

					}

					remove_dynamic_modifier = {

						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive

					}

				}

				OR = {

    chi_shaan_offensive = { #陕甘宁攻势



		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans



		allowed = {

			is_literally_china = yes

		}



		available = {

			any_of_scopes = {

				array = global.big_china

				tooltip = big_china_tt

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				custom_trigger_tooltip = {

					tooltip = is_in_strat_245

					region = 245

				}

				controller = {

					has_war_with = ROOT

				}

			}

			NOT = { has_active_mission = chi_preparing_offensive }

			any_of_scopes = {

				array = global.big_china

				tooltip = big_china_tt

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				custom_trigger_tooltip = {

					tooltip = is_in_strat_245

					region = 245

				}

				OR = {

					is_controlled_by = ROOT

					num_owned_neighbour_states = {

						owner = ROOT

						count > 0

					}

				}

			}

		}



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_states_trigger = { 

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				region = 245

			}



 			highlight_color_before_active = 3

			highlight_color_while_active = 2

		}



		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view



		cost = 0



		fire_only_once = yes



		days_remove = @offsive_days



		modifier = {

			

		}



		visible = {

			OR = {

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				AND = {

					is_ai = no

					is_literally_china = yes

					OR = {

						has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

						has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china

					}

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				}

				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag

			any_of_scopes = {

				array = global.big_china

				tooltip = big_china_tt

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				custom_trigger_tooltip = {

					tooltip = is_in_strat_245

					region = 245

				}

			}

			NOT = {

                has_active_mission = chi_shaan_offensive_mission

			}

		}



		complete_effect = {

			activate_mission = chi_preparing_offensive

			set_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag

			every_other_country = {

				limit = {

					OR = {

						tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

						tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

					}

				}

				activate_mission = chi_shaan_offensive_mission

			}

		}



		remove_effect = {

			for_each_scope_loop = {

				array = global.big_china

				if = {

					limit = {

						region = 245

					}

					clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

					remove_dynamic_modifier = {

						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive

					}

				}

			}

			#if = {

			#	limit = {

			#		has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts

			#		171 = { is_controlled_by = SPD }

			#	}

			#	add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_republican_offensive days = 30 }

			#}

		}



		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0.1

			modifier = {

				factor = 0

				OR = {

					all_of_scopes = {

						array = global.big_china

						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

						region = 245

						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	

					}

					NOT = {

						any_of_scopes = {

							array = global.big_china

							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

							region = 245

							controller = {

								has_war_with = ROOT

							}

						}

					}

				}  

			}

			#modifier = {

			#	factor = 200

			#	tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

			#}

			#modifier = {

			#	factor = 10

			#	divisions_in_state = {

			#		state = 171

			#		size > 0

			#	}

			#	NOT = {

			#		has_full_control_of_state = 171

			#	}

			#}

		}

	}

		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0.1

			modifier = {

				factor = 0

				OR = {

					all_of_scopes = {

						array = global.big_china

						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

						region = 248

						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	

					}

					NOT = {

							array = global.big_china

    chi_southwest_offensive = { #西南攻势



		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans



		allowed = {

			is_literally_china = yes

		}



		available = {

			any_of_scopes = {

				array = global.big_china

				tooltip = big_china_tt

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				custom_trigger_tooltip = {

					tooltip = is_in_strat_249

					region = 249

				}

				controller = {

					has_war_with = ROOT

				}

			}

			NOT = { has_active_mission = chi_preparing_offensive }

			any_of_scopes = {

				array = global.big_china

				tooltip = big_china_tt

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				custom_trigger_tooltip = {

					tooltip = is_in_strat_249

					region = 249

				}

				OR = {

					is_controlled_by = ROOT

					num_owned_neighbour_states = {

						owner = ROOT

						count > 0

					}

				}

			}

		}



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_states_trigger = { 

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				region = 249

			}



 			highlight_color_before_active = 3

			highlight_color_while_active = 2

		}



		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view



		cost = 0



		fire_only_once = yes



		days_remove = @offsive_days



		modifier = {

			

		}



		visible = {

			OR = {

				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				AND = {

					is_ai = no

					is_literally_china = yes

					OR = {

						has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

						has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china

					}

				}

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

				}

				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china

			}

			if = {

				limit = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				}

				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag

			any_of_scopes = {

				array = global.big_china

				tooltip = big_china_tt

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				custom_trigger_tooltip = {

					tooltip = is_in_strat_249

					region = 249

				}

			}

			NOT = {

                has_active_mission = chi_southwest_offensive_mission

			}

		}



		complete_effect = {

			activate_mission = chi_preparing_offensive

			set_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag

			every_other_country = {

				limit = {

					OR = {

						tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

						tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

					}

				}

				activate_mission = chi_southwest_offensive_mission

			}

		}



		remove_effect = {

			for_each_scope_loop = {

				array = global.big_china

				if = {

					limit = {

						region = 249

					}

					clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

					remove_dynamic_modifier = {

						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive

					}

				}

			}

			#if = {

			#	limit = {

			#		has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts

			#		171 = { is_controlled_by = SPD }

			#	}

			#	add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_republican_offensive days = 30 }

			#}

		}



		ai_will_do = {

			base = 0.1

			modifier = {

				factor = 0

				OR = {

					all_of_scopes = {

						array = global.big_china

						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

						region = 249

						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	

					}

					NOT = {

						any_of_scopes = {

							array = global.big_china

							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

							region = 249

							controller = {

								has_war_with = ROOT

							}

						}

					}

				}  

			}

			#modifier = {

			#	factor = 200

			#	tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

			#}

			#modifier = {

			#	factor = 10

			#	divisions_in_state = {

			always = no

		}



		visible = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				}

			}

			OR = {

				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			has_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag

		}



		timeout_effect = {

			clr_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag

		}

		}



		available = {

			hidden_trigger = { always = no }

		}



		highlight_states = {

			highlight_states_trigger = { 

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				region = 249

			}

 			highlight_color_before_active = 1

		}



		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view



		fire_only_once = yes



		days_mission_timeout = @offsive_days



		is_good = no



		cancel_if_not_visible = yes



		activation = {

			always = no

		}



		visible = {

			hidden_trigger = {

                OR = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china

					AND = {

						is_ai = no

						is_literally_china = yes

						OR = {

							has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

							has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china

						}

					}

				}

			}

			OR = {

				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china

				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			}

			any_of_scopes = {

				array = global.big_china

				tooltip = big_china_tt

				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

				custom_trigger_tooltip = {

					tooltip = is_in_strat_249

					region = 249

				}

			}

		}



		timeout_effect = {

			effect_tooltip = {

                for_each_scope_loop = {

					array = global.big_china

					if = {

						limit = {

							region = 249

						}

						clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

						remove_dynamic_modifier = {

							modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive

						}

					}

				}

			}

		}

	}

}

			}

		}

visible = {	

			hidden_trigger = {

				OR = {

					has_completed_focus = CHI_mongolian_and_tibetan_affairs_commission

					AND = {

						is_legit_china = yes

						NOT = {

							tag = CHI

						}

					}

					any_owned_state = {

						is_controlled_by = ROOT

						is_core_of = MON

					}

				}

			}

		}
